    23→  }, [isOpen])  // missing handleClose in deps  
    24→  ```  
    25→- **Fix:** Either wrap `handleClose` in `useCallback` and add it to the dependency array, or inline the submitting guard in the effect and add `submitting` to deps. Example: `}, [isOpen, submitting])` with an inline check.

    14→### [CC-001] Stale `agentId` closure in `requestTransfer` and `resolveTransfer` body payloads  
    15→- **File:** /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/hooks/useGovernance.ts:253, 272  
    16→- **Severity:** SHOULD-FIX  
    17→- **Category:** logic (stale closure)  
    18→- **Confidence:** CONFIRMED  
    19→- **Description:** `requestTransfer` sends `requestedBy: agentId` (line 253) and `resolveTransfer` sends `resolvedBy: agentId` (line 272). Both callbacks correctly list `agentId` in their dependency arrays (lines 263, 282), so the closure will be recreated when `agentId` changes. However, the `agentId` parameter to `useGovernance` is typed `string | null`. If `agentId` is `null` at call time, the payloads send `requestedBy: null` / `resolvedBy: null` to the server. There is no guard like the one in `useTeam.updateTeam` (`if (!teamId) return`). If the server does not validate these fields, a transfer request could be created with `requestedBy: null`.  
    20→- **Evidence:**  
    21→  ```typescript  
    22→  // line 253 — agentId may be null  
    23→  body: JSON.stringify({ agentId: targetAgentId, fromTeamId, toTeamId, requestedBy: agentId, note }),  
    24→  // line 272 — agentId may be null  
    25→  body: JSON.stringify({ action, resolvedBy: agentId, rejectReason }),  
    26→  ```  
    27→- **Fix:** Add an early-return guard at the top of both callbacks: `if (!agentId) return { success: false, error: 'No agent selected' }`. This matches the defensive pattern used in `useTeam.updateTeam` (line 44).  
    28→  
    29→### [CC-002] `refresh()` calls in mutation callbacks do not use AbortController, risking state updates after unmount  
    30→- **File:** /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/hooks/useGovernance.  

... [8737 more chars truncated]

    10→### [CC-001] TOCTOU race in transfers/route.ts POST: team state can change between validation and createTransferRequest  
    11→- **File:** /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/app/api/governance/transfers/route.ts:63-95  
    12→- **Severity:** MUST-FIX  
    13→- **Category:** race-condition  
    14→- **Confidence:** CONFIRMED  
    15→- **Description:** The POST handler reads team state (line 63: `loadTeams()`) and validates it (lines 64-86: fromTeam exists, agent is in fromTeam, toTeam exists, COS check, type check), then calls `createTransferRequest()` (line 95) which acquires a `'transfers'` lock internally. However, between the validation reads and the write, another request could modify the teams file (e.g., removing the agent from the team, deleting the team, or changing the team type from closed to open). The validation and creation are NOT atomic with respect to team state.  
    16→- **Evidence:**  
    17→```typescript  
    18→// Line 63-86: Reads and validates team state WITHOUT holding any lock  
    19→const teams = loadTeams()  
    20→const fromTeam = teams.find(t => t.id === fromTeamId)  
    21→// ... validation checks ...  
    22→if (fromTeam.type !== 'closed') { ... }  
    23→  
    24→// Line 95: Creates transfer request — acquires 'transfers' lock but NOT 'teams' lock  
    25→const transferRequest = await createTransferRequest({ agentId, fromTeamId, toTeamId, requestedBy, note })  
    26→```  
    27→- **Fix:** Wrap the entire validation + creation in a `withLock('teams', ...)` block, or at minimum re-validate team state inside the `createTransferRequest` callback (which already holds the `'transfers'` lock). Alternatively, acquire both the `'teams'` and `'transfers'` locks before validation (always in the same order to avoid deadl

Fix the following issue in `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/app/teams/page.tsx`. Read the file first.  

**CC-019 (NIT)**: The Create Team dialog only handles Escape via the input's `onKeyDown`. If the user clicks outside the input but inside the modal overlay, pressing Escape won't close the dialog.  

Fix: Add a `useEffect` that listens for Escape at the document level when the create dialog is open:  
```tsx
useEffect(() => {
  if (!showCreateDialog) return
  const handleKey = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
    if (e.key === 'Escape') setShowCreateDialog(false)
  }
  document.addEventListener('keydown', handleKey)
  return () => document.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKey)
}, [showCreateDialog])
```

Find the appropriate state variable name for the create dialog visibility (it may be `showCreate`, `isCreating`, `showCreateDialog`, etc.) and use that.

    41→    return parsed  
    42→  } catch (error) {  
    43→    // Distinguish read errors from parse errors — parse errors indicate disk corruption  
    44→    if (error instanceof SyntaxError) {

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #FF9800; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

The CC-015 test correctly found a real bug: `isManager(null)` returns `true` when `managerId` is also `null` because `null === null` is `true` in JavaScript. **Result:**

     1→/**  
     2→ * Simple in-memory rate limiter for governance password operations.  
     3→ * Tracks failed attempts per key with a fixed time window.  
     4→ * Phase 1 only — no distributed state needed for localhost.  
     5→ */  
     6→  
     7→const limits = new Map<string, { count: number; resetAt: number }>()  
     8→  
     9→const DEFAULT_MAX_ATTEMPTS = 5  
    10→const DEFAULT_WINDOW_MS = 60_000 // 1 minute  
    11→  
    12→/** Check if the rate limit allows another attempt */  
    13→export function checkRateLimit(  
    14→  key: string,  
    15→  maxAttempts: number = DEFAULT_MAX_ATTEMPTS,  
    16→  windowMs: number = DEFAULT_WINDOW_MS  
    17→): { allowed: boolean; retryAfterMs: number } {  
    18→  const now = Date.now()  
    19→  const entry = limits.get(key)  
    20→  
    21→  // Window expired — reset  
    22→  if (entry && now >= entry.resetAt) {  
    23→    limits.delete(key)  
    24→    return { allowed: true, retryAfterMs: 0 }  
    25→  }  
    26→  
    27→  // Check if over limit  
    28→  if (entry && entry.count >= maxAttempts) {  
    29→    return { allowed: false, retryAfterMs: entry.resetAt - now }  
    30→  }  
    31→  
    32→  return { allowed: true, retryAfterMs: 0 }  
    33→}  
    34→  
    35→/** Record a failed attempt */  
    36→export function recordFailure(key: string, windowMs: number = DEFAULT_WINDOW_MS): void {  
    37→  let entry = limits.get(key)  
    38→  const now = Date.now()  
    39→  // Reset expired windows so stale counts are not reused  
    40→  if (entry && now >= entry.resetAt) { entry = undefined; limits.delete(key) }  
    41→  const fresh = entry || { count: 0, resetAt: now + windowMs }  
    42→  limits.set(key, { count: fresh.count + 1, resetAt: fresh.resetAt })  
    43→}  
    44→  
    45→/** Reset rate limit on successful attempt */  
    46→export function resetRateLimit(key: string): void {  
    47→  limits.delete(key)  
    48→}  
    49→  
    50→// Periodic cleanup to prevent Map from growing unbounded  
    51→// (defensive — governance operations are infrequ  

... [464 more chars truncated]

**Result:**

     1→/**  
     2→ * File Lock — in-process mutex for serializing load→modify→save operations  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Prevents concurrent read-modify-write races within a single Node.js process.  
     5→ * Each registry file gets its own named lock. When one API request is mid-write,  
     6→ * other requests for the same file queue up and run sequentially.  
     7→ *  
     8→ * This is sufficient for Phase 1 (single Next.js process, localhost).  
     9→ * For multi-process deployments, replace with advisory file locks (e.g., proper-lockfile).  
    10→ */  
    11→  
    12→/**  
    13→ * LOCK ORDERING INVARIANT:  
    14→ * When acquiring multiple locks, always acquire in this order:  
    15→ *   1. 'teams'  
    16→ *   2. 'transfers'  
    17→ *   3. 'governance'  
    18→ * Violating this order will cause deadlock.  
    19→ *  
    20→ * Current nested lock usage:  
    21→ * - transfers/[id]/resolve/route.ts: acquires 'teams' then 'transfers' (via resolveTransferRequest)  
    22→ */  
    23→  
    24→// Map of lock name -> queue of pending resolve callbacks  
    25→const locks = new Map<string, Array<() => void>>()  
    26→// Set of currently held lock names  
    27→const held = new Set<string>()  
    28→  
    29→/**  
    30→ * Acquire a named lock. Returns a release function.  
    31→ * If the lock is already held, the caller awaits until it is released.  
    32→ */  
    33→export function acquireLock(name: string): Promise<() => void> {  
    34→  if (!held.has(name)) {  
    35→    // Lock is free — acquire immediately  
    36→    held.add(name)  
    37→    return Promise.resolve(() => releaseLock(name))  
    38→  }  
    39→  
    40→  // Lock is held — enqueue and wait  
    41→  return new Promise<() => void>((resolve) => {  
    42→    if (!locks.has(name)) {  
    43→      locks.set(name, [])  
    44→    }  
    45→    locks.get(name)!.push(() => {  
    46→      resolve(() => releaseLock(name))  
    47→    })  
    48→  })  
    49→}  
    50→  
    51→/**  
    52→ * Release a named lock and wake the next waiter if any.  
    

... [894 more chars truncated]  

</details>

Fix ALL the following issues in `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/components/MessageCenter.tsx`. Read the file first.  

1. **CC-003 (MUST-FIX)**: `sendMessage` uses `sessionName` for the `from` field but `messageIdentifier` for everything else. Find where `from: sessionName` is set in the send message function and change it to `from: messageIdentifier` for consistency.  

2. **CC-002 (MUST-FIX)**: Wrap `loadMessage` in `useCallback` with dependencies on `messageIdentifier` and `apiBaseUrl` (or whatever variables it closes over).  

3. **CC-008 (SHOULD-FIX)**: `showToast` uses `setTimeout` without cleanup. Store the timeout ID in a `useRef` and clear it on unmount and on each new call:  
   - Add `const toastTimerRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null)`   
   - In `showToast`, clear previous: `if (toastTimerRef.current) clearTimeout(toastTimerRef.current)` then `toastTimerRef.current = setTimeout(...)`  
   - Add a cleanup useEffect that clears on unmount  

4. **CC-009 (SHOULD-FIX)**: Same pattern for `deleteMessage` confirmation timeout — `setPendingDelete(null)` timeout. Store in a ref, clear on unmount and on each new call.  

5. **CC-010 (SHOULD-FIX)**: Add `role="option"` to each suggestion item div in the autocomplete listbox. Find divs inside the container that has `role="listbox"` and add `role="option"` to each child item.  

6. **CC-016 (NIT)**: `sentCount` state is maintained but never displayed. Remove the `sentCount` state, the `fetchSentCount` function, and calls to it. This eliminates unnecessary API requests.  

7. **CC-021 (NIT)**: The compose form message label is not associated with the textarea. Find `<label>` before `<textarea id="compose-message"` and add `htmlFor="compose-message"` to the label.

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 18:00:45]*

<summary>🔧 Tool: Edit -- `MessageCenter.tsx`</summary>

**Old:**  
```
  // Load message details
  const loadMessage = async (messageId: string, box: 'inbox' | 'sent' = 'inbox') => {
    try {
      const response = await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/api/messages?agent=${encodeURIComponent(messageIdentifier)}&id=${messageId}&box=${box}`)
      if (!response.ok) return
      const message = await response.json()
      setSelectedMessage(message)

      // Mark as read if unread (inbox only)
      if (box === 'inbox' && message.status === 'unread') {
        await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/api/messages?agent=${encodeURIComponent(messageIdentifier)}&id=${messageId}&action=read`, {
          method: 'PATCH',
        })
        fetchMessages()
        fetchUnreadCount()
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error loading message:', error)
    }
  }
```

**New:**  
```
  // Load message details
  const loadMessage = useCallback(async (messageId: string, box: 'inbox' | 'sent' = 'inbox') => {
    try {
      const response = await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/api/messages?agent=${encodeURIComponent(messageIdentifier)}&id=${messageId}&box=${box}`)
      if (!response.ok) return
      const message = await response.json()
      setSelectedMessage(message)

      // Mark as read if unread (inbox only)
      if (box === 'inbox' && message.status === 'unread') {
        await fetch(`${apiBaseUrl}/api/messages?agent=${encodeURIComponent(messageIdentifier)}&id=${messageId}&action=read`, {
          method: 'PATCH',
        })
        fetchMessages()
        fetchUnreadCount()
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error loading message:', error)
    }
  }, [messageIdentifier, apiBaseUrl, fetchMessages, fetchUnreadCount])
```

**Result:**

The file /Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/components/MessageCenter.tsx has been updated successfully.

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 18:00:53]*

<details>
<summary>🔧 Tool: Edit -- `MessageCenter.tsx`</summary>

**Input:**

**File:** `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/components/MessageCenter.tsx`  

**Old:**  
```
  // Toast notification state (replaces native alert/confirm)
  const [toast, setToast] = useState<{ message: string; type: 'success' | 'error' | 'info' } | null>(null)
  const [pendingDelete, setPendingDelete] = useState<string | null>(null)

  // Show a toast notification that auto-dismisses
  const showToast = useCallback((message: string, type: 'success' | 'error' | 'info' = 'info') => {
    setToast({ message, type })
    setTimeout(() => setToast(null), 3000)
  }, [])
```

**New:**  
```
  // Toast notification state (replaces native alert/confirm)
  const [toast, setToast] = useState<{ message: string; type: 'success' | 'error' | 'info' } | null>(null)
  const [pendingDelete, setPendingDelete] = useState<string | null>(null)
  const toastTimerRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null)
  const deleteTimerRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null)

  // Show a toast notification that auto-dismisses
  const showToast = useCallback((message: string, type: 'success' | 'error' | 'info' = 'info') => {
    if (toastTimerRef.current) clearTimeout(toastTimerRef.current)
    setToast({ message, type })
    toastTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => setToast(null), 3000)
  }, [])

  // Cleanup toast and delete confirmation timers on unmount
  useEffect(() => {
    return () => {
      if (toastTimerRef.current) clearTimeout(toastTimerRef.current)
      if (deleteTimerRef.current) clearTimeout(deleteTimerRef.current)
    }
  }, [])
```

     5→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {  
     6→  try {  
     7→    let body  
     8→    try { body = await request.json() } catch {  
     9→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid JSON body' }, { status: 400 })  
    10→    }  
    11→    const { password, currentPassword } = body  
    12→  
    13→    if (!password || typeof password !== 'string' || password.length < 6) {  
    14→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Password must be at least 6 characters' }, { status: 400 })  
    15→    }  
    16→    if (password.length > 72) {  
    17→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Password must not exceed 72 characters (bcrypt limit)' }, { status: 400 })  
    18→    }  
    19→  
    20→    const config = loadGovernance()  
    21→  
    22→    // If password already set, require current password  
    23→    if (config.passwordHash) {  
    24→      // Rate limit password verification to prevent brute-force attacks  
    25→      const rateCheck = checkRateLimit('governance-password-change')  
    26→      if (!rateCheck.allowed) {  
    27→        return NextResponse.json(  
    28→          { error: `Too many failed password attempts. Try again in ${Math.ceil(rateCheck.retryAfterMs / 1000)}s` },  
    29→          { status: 429 }  
    30→        )  
    31→      }  
    32→  
    33→      if (!currentPassword || !(await verifyPassword(currentPassword))) {  
    34→        recordFailure('governance-password-change')  
    35→        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid current password' }, { status: 401 })  
    36→      }  
    37→      // Password verified successfully — reset rate limit counter  
    38→      resetRateLimit('governance-password-change')

     1→import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server'  
     2→import { checkMessageAllowed } from '@/lib/message-filter'  
     3→import { loadAgents } from '@/lib/agent-registry'  
     4→  
     5→// In-memory cache: avoids re-reading governance + teams files for every agent  
     6→// on each request. TTL of 5 seconds balances freshness with performance.  
     7→const cache = new Map<string, { ids: string[]; expiresAt: number }>()  
     8→const CACHE_TTL_MS = 5_000  
     9→  
    10→export async function GET(request: NextRequest) {  
    11→  try {  
    12→    const agentId = request.nextUrl.searchParams.get('agentId')  
    13→  
    14→    if (!agentId) {  
    15→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'agentId query parameter is required' }, { status: 400 })  
    16→    }  
    17→  
    18→    if (agentId && typeof agentId === 'string' && !/^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+$/.test(agentId)) {  
    19→      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid agentId format' }, { status: 400 })  
    20→    }  
    21→  
    22→    // Check cache first  
    23→    const cached = cache.get(agentId)  
    24→    if (cached && Date.now() < cached.expiresAt) {  
    25→      return NextResponse.json({ reachableAgentIds: cached.ids })  
    26→    }  
    27→  
    28→    // Cache miss or expired — compute reachable agents  
    29→    const allAgents = loadAgents()  
    30→    const reachableAgentIds: string[] = []  
    31→  
    32→    for (const agent of allAgents) {  
    33→      if (agent.id === agentId) continue  
    34→      if (agent.deletedAt) continue  
    35→  
    36→      const result = checkMessageAllowed({  
    37→        senderAgentId: agentId,  
    38→        recipientAgentId: agent.id,  
    39→      })  
    40→  
    41→      if (result.allowed) {  
    42→        reachableAgentIds.push(agent.id)  
    43→      }  
    44→    }  
    45→  
    46→    // Store in cache with TTL  
    47→    cache.set(agentId, { ids: reachableAgentIds, expiresAt: Date.now() + CACHE_TTL_MS })  
    48→  
    49→    // Evict stale/expired entries on every cache   

... [466 more chars truncated]

## <span style="color:#2196F3">◆ USER</span>  *[2026-02-19 17:59:42]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #2196F3; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

Fix the following issue in `/Users/emanuelesabetta/ai-maestro/app/teams/page.tsx`. Read the file first.  

**CC-019 (NIT)**: The Create Team dialog only handles Escape via the input's `onKeyDown`. If the user clicks outside the input but inside the modal overlay, pressing Escape won't close the dialog.  

Fix: Add a `useEffect` that listens for Escape at the document level when the create dialog is open:  
```tsx
useEffect(() => {
  if (!showCreateDialog) return
  const handleKey = (e: KeyboardEvent) => {
    if (e.key === 'Escape') setShowCreateDialog(false)
  }
  document.addEventListener('keydown', handleKey)
  return () => document.removeEventListener('keydown', handleKey)
}, [showCreateDialog])
```

Find the appropriate state variable name for the create dialog visibility (it may be `showCreate`, `isCreating`, `showCreateDialog`, etc.) and use that.

```
  // Pre-load all team and agent names when Create dialog opens (for real-time collision checking)
  useEffect(() => {
    if (creating) {

        .then(res => res.ok ? res.json() : { teamNames: [], agentNames: [] })
        .then(data => setReservedNames(data))
        .catch(() => setReservedNames({ teamNames: [], agentNames: [] }))
```

export function updateTask(  
  teamId: string,  
  taskId: string,  
  updates: Partial<Pick<Task, 'subject' | 'description' | 'status' | 'assigneeAgentId' | 'blockedBy' | 'priority'>>  
): Promise<{ task: Task | null; unblocked: Task[] }> {  
  return withLock('tasks-' + teamId, () => {  
    const tasks = loadTasks(teamId)  
    const index = tasks.findIndex(t => t.id === taskId)  
    if (index === -1) return { task: null, unblocked: [] }  

    const now = new Date().toISOString()  
    const wasCompleted = tasks[index].status === 'completed'  
    const isNowCompleted = updates.status === 'completed'  

    tasks[index] = {  
      ...tasks[index],  
      ...updates,  
      updatedAt: now,

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 18:06:58]*

<summary>🔧 Tool: Bash -- Fix type-safe updates object construction</summary>

**Input:**

*Fix type-safe updates object construction*  

```bash
python3 << 'PYEOF'
import pathlib

filepath = pathlib.Path("app/api/teams/[id]/tasks/[taskId]/route.ts")
content = filepath.read_text()

old = """    const result = await updateTask(id, taskId, {
      subject,
      description,
      status,
      assigneeAgentId,
      blockedBy,
      priority,
    })"""

new = """    // Build typed updates object — all fields were validated above so casts are safe
    const updates: Partial<Pick<import('@/types/task').Task, 'subject' | 'description' | 'status' | 'assigneeAgentId' | 'blockedBy' | 'priority'>> = {}
    if (typeof subject === 'string') updates.subject = subject
    if (typeof description === 'string') updates.description = description
    if (typeof status === 'string') updates.status = status as import('@/types/task').Task['status']
    if (typeof assigneeAgentId === 'string') updates.assigneeAgentId = assigneeAgentId
    if (Array.isArray(blockedBy)) updates.blockedBy = blockedBy as string[]
    if (typeof priority === 'number') updates.priority = priority
    const result = await updateTask(id, taskId, updates)"""

if old not in content:
    print("ERROR: target block not found")
else:
    content = content.replace(old, new)
    filepath.write_text(content)
    print("OK: replaced updateTask call")
PYEOF
```

     5→export async function POST(request: NextRequest) {

     1→'use client'  
     2→  
     3→import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react'  
     4→import type { Team } from '@/types/team'  
     5→  
     6→interface UseTeamResult {  
     7→  team: Team | null  
     8→  loading: boolean  
     9→  error: string | null  
    10→  updateTeam: (updates: { name?: string; description?: string; agentIds?: string[]; instructions?: string }) => Promise<void>  
    11→  refreshTeam: () => Promise<void>  
    12→}  
    13→  
    14→export function useTeam(teamId: string | null): UseTeamResult {  
    15→  const [team, setTeam] = useState<Team | null>(null)  
    16→  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(!!teamId)  // Start true only when teamId is provided, preventing "Team not found" flash  
    17→  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null)  
    18→  
    19→  const fetchTeam = useCallback(async () => {  
    20→    if (!teamId) return  
    21→    try {  
    22→      const res = await fetch(`/api/teams/${teamId}`)  
    23→      if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Failed to fetch team')  
    24→      const data = await res.json()  
    25→      setTeam(data.team || null)  
    26→      setError(null)  
    27→    } catch (err) {  
    28→      setError(err instanceof Error ? err.message : 'Failed to fetch team')  
    29→    }  
    30→  }, [teamId])  
    31→  
    32→  // Initial fetch  
    33→  useEffect(() => {  
    34→    if (!teamId) {  
    35→      setTeam(null)  
    36→      setLoading(false)  
    37→      return  
    38→    }  
    39→    setLoading(true)  
    40→    fetchTeam().finally(() => setLoading(false))  
    41→  }, [teamId, fetchTeam])  
    42→  
    43→  const updateTeam = useCallback(async (updates: { name?: string; description?: string; agentIds?: string[]; instructions?: string }) => {  
    44→    if (!teamId) return  
    45→    // Optimistic update  
    46→    setTeam(prev => prev ? { ...prev, ...updates, updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() } : prev)  
    47→    try {

     1→/**  
     2→ * Message Filter — enforces closed-team messaging isolation  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Determines whether a message from sender to recipient is allowed  
     5→ * based on governance roles (MANAGER, Chief-of-Staff) and closed-team  
     6→ * membership. Open-world agents (not in any closed team) can message  
     7→ * freely unless the recipient is inside a closed team.  
     8→ */  
     9→

    11→import { loadTeams } from './team-registry'  
    12→  
    13→export interface MessageFilterInput {  
    14→  senderAgentId: string | null // null = mesh-forwarded message  
    15→  recipientAgentId: string  
    16→}  
    17→  
    18→export interface MessageFilterResult {  
    19→  allowed: boolean  
    20→  reason?: string  
    21→}  
    22→  
    23→/**  
    24→ * Check whether a message from sender to recipient is allowed.  
    25→ *  
    26→ * Algorithm (R6.1–R6.7):  
    27→ * 1. Mesh-forwarded (senderAgentId null): denied if recipient is in a closed team (unverified sender)  
    28→ * 1b. Unresolved recipient (alias, not UUID) from closed-team sender: denied (prevents bypass)  
    29→ * 2. Neither in a closed team: allowed (open world, current behavior) (R6.4)  
    30→ * 3. Sender is MANAGER: always allowed (R6.3)  
    31→ * 4. Sender is COS of any closed team: can reach MANAGER, other COS, own team members (R6.2)  
    32→ * 5. Normal closed-team member: can reach same-team members and own COS (R6.1)  
    33→ * 6. Outside sender to closed-team recipient: denied (R6.5) — always reached after Steps 2–5  
    34→ *  
    35→ * IMPORTANT (R6.7): Uses getClosedTeamsForAgent (plural) to correctly handle  
    36→ * COS agents who belong to multiple closed teams simultaneously.  
    37→ */

## <span style="color:#FF9800">◈ SUB-AGENT</span>  *[2026-02-19 18:01:47]*

<div style="border-left: 4px solid #FF9800; padding-left: 12px; margin: 4px 0;">

I see the issue. The existing tests use non-UUID agent IDs like `cos-alpha`, `member-a1`, etc. The implementation at line 62-68 has a UUID check: `/^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}/`. Since these are plain strings (not UUIDs), Step 1b kicks in and denies messages from closed-team senders to non-UUID recipients before reaching the COS/member logic.  

This means the **existing tests were already broken before my changes**. My 3 new tests (2 pass, 1 fails for the same reason) are affected by this pre-existing issue. Let me verify this is a pre-existing problem by checking the original test.  

The root cause: The existing tests use non-UUID-like agent IDs (e.g., `cos-alpha`, `member-a1`), but the implementation's Step 1b denies messages from closed-team senders to non-UUID recipients. The tests were written before Step 1b was added, or Step 1b was added after the tests.  

The fix is to use UUID-like agent IDs in all tests. Let me update the entire test file to use UUID-like IDs.  

</div>

// ============================================================================
// CC-007: 400 validation paths for missing/invalid fields
// ============================================================================

describe('CC-007: request body validation', () => {
  it('returns 400 when action is missing', async () => {
    /** Verifies that the route rejects requests where the action field is absent */
    const req = makeRequest({ resolvedBy: 'cos-source' })
    const res = await POST(req, makeParams('tr-1'))
    const data = await res.json()

    expect(res.status).toBe(400)
    expect(data.error).toContain('action and resolvedBy are required')
  })

  it('returns 400 when resolvedBy is missing', async () => {
    /** Verifies that the route rejects requests where the resolvedBy field is absent */
    const req = makeRequest({ action: 'approve' })
    const res = await POST(req, makeParams('tr-1'))
    const data = await res.json()

    expect(res.status).toBe(400)
    expect(data.error).toContain('action and resolvedBy are required')
  })

  it('returns 400 when action is invalid', async () => {
    /** Verifies that the route rejects requests where action is not "approve" or "reject" */
    const req = makeRequest({ action: 'invalid', resolvedBy: 'cos-source' })
    const res = await POST(req, makeParams('tr-1'))
    const data = await res.json()

    expect(res.status).toBe(400)
    expect(data.error).toContain('action must be "approve" or "reject"')
  })
})

     1→/**  
     2→ * Document Registry - File-based CRUD for team document persistence  
     3→ *  
     4→ * Storage: ~/.aimaestro/teams/docs-{teamId}.json (one per team)  
     5→ * Mirrors the pattern from lib/task-registry.ts  
     6→ */  
     7→  
     8→import fs from 'fs'  
     9→import path from 'path'  
    10→import os from 'os'  
    11→import { v4 as uuidv4 } from 'uuid'  
    12→import { withLock } from '@/lib/file-lock'  
    13→import type { TeamDocument, TeamDocumentsFile } from '@/types/document'  
    14→  
    15→const TEAMS_DIR = path.join(os.homedir(), '.aimaestro', 'teams')  
    16→  
    17→function ensureTeamsDir() {  
    18→  if (!fs.existsSync(TEAMS_DIR)) {  
    19→    fs.mkdirSync(TEAMS_DIR, { recursive: true })  
    20→  }  
    21→}  
    22→  
    23→function docsFilePath(teamId: string): string {  
    24→  return path.join(TEAMS_DIR, `docs-${teamId}.json`)  
    25→}  
    26→  
    27→export function loadDocuments(teamId: string): TeamDocument[] {  
    28→  try {  
    29→    ensureTeamsDir()  
    30→    const filePath = docsFilePath(teamId)  
    31→    if (!fs.existsSync(filePath)) {  
    32→      return []  
    33→    }  
    34→    const data = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8')  
    35→    const parsed: TeamDocumentsFile = JSON.parse(data)  
    36→    return Array.isArray(parsed.documents) ? parsed.documents : []  
    37→  } catch (error) {  
    38→    console.error(`Failed to load documents for team ${teamId}:`, error)  
    39→    return []  
    40→  }  
    41→}  
    42→  
    43→export function saveDocuments(teamId: string, documents: TeamDocument[]): boolean {  
    44→  try {  
    45→    ensureTeamsDir()  
    46→    const file: TeamDocumentsFile = { version: 1, documents }  
    47→    fs.writeFileSync(docsFilePath(teamId), JSON.stringify(file, null, 2), 'utf-8')  
    48→    return true  
    49→  } catch (error) {  
    50→    console.error(`Failed to save documents for team ${teamId}:`, error)  
    51→    return false  
    52→  }  
    53→}  
    54→  
    55→export function getDocument(teamId: string,
